00033 /********************************************************************
00034 *
00035 * Standard register and bit definitions for the Texas Instruments
00036 * MSP430 microcontroller.
00037 *
00038 * This file supports assembler and C development for
00039 * CC430x613x devices.
00040 *
00041 * Texas Instruments, Version 1.9
00042 *
00043 * Rev. 1.0, First Release
00044 * Rev. 1.1, added TLV definitions
00045 * Rev. 1.2, added some more DMA Trigger definitions
00046 * Rev. 1.3, fixed LCDMEM access
00047 * Rev. 1.4, changed RTC_A_VECTOR to RTC_VECTOR
00048 * Rev. 1.5, clean up of Flash section
00049 * Rev. 1.6, Changed access type of DMAxSZ registers to word only
00050 * Rev. 1.7  Changed access type of TimerA/B registers to word only
00051 * Rev. 1.8  Removed not available Definitions: RF1AIFIV_RFRXIFG and RF1AIFIV_TFRXIFG
00052 * Rev. 1.9  Removed not available Definitions: CRCDIRB and CRCRESR
00053 *
00054 *
00055 ********************************************************************/
00056

00071 #ifndef SFR_8BIT
00072 /* External references resolved by a device-specific linker command file */
00073 #define SFR_8BIT(address)   extern volatile unsigned char address
00074 #define SFR_16BIT(address)  extern volatile unsigned int address
00075 //#define SFR_20BIT(address)  extern volatile unsigned int address
00076 typedef void (* __SFR_FARPTR)();
00077 #define SFR_20BIT(address) extern __SFR_FARPTR address
00078 #define SFR_32BIT(address)  extern volatile unsigned long address
00079 
00080 #endif

00118 /* Low Power Modes coded with Bits 4-7 in SR */
00119 
00120 #ifdef __ASM_HEADER__ /* Begin #defines for assembler */
00121 #define LPM0                   (CPUOFF)
00122 #define LPM1                   (SCG0+CPUOFF)
00123 #define LPM2                   (SCG1+CPUOFF)
00124 #define LPM3                   (SCG1+SCG0+CPUOFF)
00125 #define LPM4                   (SCG1+SCG0+OSCOFF+CPUOFF)
00126 /* End #defines for assembler */
00127 
00128 #else /* Begin #defines for C */
00129 #define LPM0_bits              (CPUOFF)
00130 #define LPM1_bits              (SCG0+CPUOFF)
00131 #define LPM2_bits              (SCG1+CPUOFF)
00132 #define LPM3_bits              (SCG1+SCG0+CPUOFF)
00133 #define LPM4_bits              (SCG1+SCG0+OSCOFF+CPUOFF)
00134 
00135 #include "in430.h"
00136 #include <intrinsics.h>
00137 
00138 #define LPM0      __bis_SR_register(LPM0_bits)         /* Enter Low Power Mode 0 */
00139 #define LPM0_EXIT __bic_SR_register_on_exit(LPM0_bits) /* Exit Low Power Mode 0 */
00140 #define LPM1      __bis_SR_register(LPM1_bits)         /* Enter Low Power Mode 1 */
00141 #define LPM1_EXIT __bic_SR_register_on_exit(LPM1_bits) /* Exit Low Power Mode 1 */
00142 #define LPM2      __bis_SR_register(LPM2_bits)         /* Enter Low Power Mode 2 */
00143 #define LPM2_EXIT __bic_SR_register_on_exit(LPM2_bits) /* Exit Low Power Mode 2 */
00144 #define LPM3      __bis_SR_register(LPM3_bits)         /* Enter Low Power Mode 3 */
00145 #define LPM3_EXIT __bic_SR_register_on_exit(LPM3_bits) /* Exit Low Power Mode 3 */
00146 #define LPM4      __bis_SR_register(LPM4_bits)         /* Enter Low Power Mode 4 */
00147 #define LPM4_EXIT __bic_SR_register_on_exit(LPM4_bits) /* Exit Low Power Mode 4 */
00148 #endif /* End #defines for C */

01016 
01017 SFR_16BIT(RF1AIFCTL0);                        /* Radio interface control register 0 */
01018 SFR_8BIT(RF1AIFCTL0_L);                       /* Radio interface control register 0 */
01019 SFR_8BIT(RF1AIFCTL0_H);                       /* Radio interface control register 0 */
01020 SFR_16BIT(RF1AIFCTL1);                        /* Radio interface control register 1 */
01021 SFR_8BIT(RF1AIFCTL1_L);                       /* Radio interface control register 1 */
01022 SFR_8BIT(RF1AIFCTL1_H);                       /* Radio interface control register 1 */
01023 #define  RF1AIFIFG             RF1AIFCTL1_L   /* Radio interface interrupt flag register */
01024 #define  RF1AIFIE              RF1AIFCTL1_H   /* Radio interface interrupt enable register */
01025 SFR_16BIT(RF1AIFCTL2);                        /* (Radio interface control register 2) */
01026 SFR_8BIT(RF1AIFCTL2_L);                       /* (Radio interface control register 2) */
01027 SFR_8BIT(RF1AIFCTL2_H);                       /* (Radio interface control register 2) */
01028 SFR_16BIT(RF1AIFERR);                         /* Radio interface error flag register */
01029 SFR_8BIT(RF1AIFERR_L);                        /* Radio interface error flag register */

01194 // Radio Core Registers
01195 #define IOCFG2                 0x00           /*  IOCFG2   - GDO2 output pin configuration  */

01207 #define FSCTRL0                0x0C           /*  FSCTRL0  - Frequency synthesizer control */

01213 #define MDMCFG2                0x12           /*  MDMCFG2  - Modem configuration */
01214 #define MDMCFG1                0x13           /*  MDMCFG1  - Modem configuration */
01215 #define MDMCFG0                0x14           /*  MDMCFG0  - Modem configuration */
01216 #define DEVIATN                0x15           /*  DEVIATN  - Modem deviation setting */
01217 #define MCSM2                  0x16           /*  MCSM2    - Main Radio Control State Machine configuration */
01218 #define MCSM1                  0x17           /*  MCSM1    - Main Radio Control State Machine configuration */
01219 #define MCSM0                  0x18           /*  MCSM0    - Main Radio Control State Machine configuration */
01220 #define FOCCFG                 0x19           /*  FOCCFG   - Frequency Offset Compensation configuration */
01221 #define BSCFG                  0x1A           /*  BSCFG    - Bit Synchronization configuration */
01222 #define AGCCTRL2               0x1B           /*  AGCCTRL2 - AGC control */

01232 #define FSCAL1                 0x25           /*  FSCAL1   - Frequency synthesizer calibration */
01233 #define FSCAL0                 0x26           /*  FSCAL0   - Frequency synthesizer calibration */

01251 #define WORTIME0               0x37           /*  WORTIME0    Low byte of WOR time */

01262 /* Radio Core Instructions */
01263 /* command strobes               */
01264 #define RF_SRES                0x30           /*  SRES    - Reset chip. */
01265 #define RF_SFSTXON             0x31           /*  SFSTXON - Enable and calibrate frequency synthesizer. */
01266 #define RF_SXOFF               0x32           /*  SXOFF   - Turn off crystal oscillator. */
01267 #define RF_SCAL                0x33           /*  SCAL    - Calibrate frequency synthesizer and turn it off. */
01268 #define RF_SRX                 0x34           /*  SRX     - Enable RX. Perform calibration if enabled. */
01269 #define RF_STX                 0x35           /*  STX     - Enable TX. If in RX state, only enable TX if CCA passes. */
01270 #define RF_SIDLE               0x36           /*  SIDLE   - Exit RX / TX, turn off frequency synthesizer. */
01271 //#define RF_SRSVD            0x37      /*  SRVSD   - Reserved.  Do not use. */
01272 #define RF_SWOR                0x38           /*  SWOR    - Start automatic RX polling sequence (Wake-on-Radio) */
01273 #define RF_SPWD                0x39           /*  SPWD    - Enter power down mode when CSn goes high. */
01274 #define RF_SFRX                0x3A           /*  SFRX    - Flush the RX FIFO buffer. */
01275 #define RF_SFTX                0x3B           /*  SFTX    - Flush the TX FIFO buffer. */
01276 #define RF_SWORRST             0x3C           /*  SWORRST - Reset real time clock. */
01277 #define RF_SNOP                0x3D           /*  SNOP    - No operation. Returns status byte. */
01278 
01279 #define RF_RXSTAT              0x80           /* Used in combination with strobe commands delivers number of availabe bytes in RX FIFO with return status */
01280 #define RF_TXSTAT              0x00           /* Used in combination with strobe commands delivers number of availabe bytes in TX FIFO with return status */

01737 //#define RESERVED            (0x0080)  /* Reserved */

01745 #define EMEX_L                 (0x0020)       /* Flash Emergency Exit */

02403 #define MPYM1                  (0x0020)       /* Multiplier mode Bit:1 */
02404 #define OP1_32                 (0x0040)       /* Bit-width of operand 1 0:16Bit / 1:32Bit */
02405 #define OP2_32                 (0x0080)       /* Bit-width of operand 2 0:16Bit / 1:32Bit */

03692 SFR_16BIT(TA0CCR0);                           /*   // Internal timer output (10.5 kHz) to Radio TX
03693   // NOTE: SMARTF_CC430 IOCFG0 should = 0x2E. When IOCFG0 = 0x2D,
03694   // asynchronous data into the radio is taken from GDO0 and not the timer.
03695   TA1CCR0 = 50;
03696   TA1CCR1 = 50;
03697 
03698   TA1CCTL0 = OUTMOD_4;
03699   TA1CCTL1 = OUTMOD_4;
03700   TA1CTL = TASSEL__SMCLK + MC_1 + TACLR; Capture/Compare 0 */

03708 /* TAxCTL Control Bits */
03709 #define TASSEL1                (0x0200)       /* Timer A clock source select 1 */
03710 #define TASSEL0                (0x0100)       /* Timer A clock source select 0 */
03711 #define ID1                    (0x0080)       /* Timer A clock input divider 1 */
03712 #define ID0                    (0x0040)       /* Timer A clock input divider 0 */
03713 #define MC1                    (0x0020)       /* Timer A mode control 1 */
03714 #define MC0                    (0x0010)       /* Timer A mode control 0 */
03715 #define TACLR                  (0x0004)       /* Timer A counter clear */
03716 #define TAIE                   (0x0002)       /* Timer A counter interrupt enable */
03717 #define TAIFG                  (0x0001)       /* Timer A counter interrupt flag */
03718 
03719 #define MC_0                   (0*0x10u)      /* Timer A mode control: 0 - Stop */
03720 #define MC_1                   (1*0x10u)      /* Timer A mode control: 1 - Up to CCR0 */
03721 #define MC_2                   (2*0x10u)      /* Timer A mode control: 2 - Continuous up */
03722 #define MC_3                   (3*0x10u)      /* Timer A mode control: 3 - Up/Down */
03723 #define ID_0                   (0*0x40u)      /* Timer A input divider: 0 - /1 */
03724 #define ID_1                   (1*0x40u)      /* Timer A input divider: 1 - /2 */
03725 #define ID_2                   (2*0x40u)      /* Timer A input divider: 2 - /4 */
03726 #define ID_3                   (3*0x40u)      /* Timer A input divider: 3 - /8 */
03727 #define TASSEL_0               (0*0x100u)     /* Timer A clock source select: 0 - TACLK */
03728 #define TASSEL_1               (1*0x100u)     /* Timer A clock source select: 1 - ACLK  */
03729 #define TASSEL_2               (2*0x100u)     /* Timer A clock source select: 2 - SMCLK */
03730 #define TASSEL_3               (3*0x100u)     /* Timer A clock source select: 3 - INCLK */
03731 #define MC__STOP               (0*0x10u)      /* Timer A mode control: 0 - Stop */
03732 #define MC__UP                 (1*0x10u)      /* Timer A mode control: 1 - Up to CCR0 */
03733 #define MC__CONTINUOUS         (2*0x10u)      /* Timer A mode control: 2 - Continuous up */
03734 #define MC__CONTINOUS          (2*0x10u)      /* Legacy define */
03735 #define MC__UPDOWN             (3*0x10u)      /* Timer A mode control: 3 - Up/Down */

04408 #define __MSP430_HAS_USCI_A0__                /* Definition to show that Module is available */

04410 #define USCI_A0_BASE           __MSP430_BASEADDRESS_USCI_A0__
04411 
04412 SFR_16BIT(UCA0CTLW0);                         /* USCI A0 Control Word Register 0 */
04413 SFR_8BIT(UCA0CTLW0_L);                        /* USCI A0 Control Word Register 0 */
04414 SFR_8BIT(UCA0CTLW0_H);                        /* USCI A0 Control Word Register 0 */
04415 #define UCA0CTL1               UCA0CTLW0_L    /* USCI A0 Control Register 1 */
04416 #define UCA0CTL0               UCA0CTLW0_H    /* USCI A0 Control Register 0 */

04418 SFR_8BIT(UCA0BRW_L);                          /* USCI A0 Baud Word Rate 0 */

04701 /************************************************************
04702 * WATCHDOG TIMER A
04703 ************************************************************/
04704 #define __MSP430_HAS_WDT_A__                  /* Definition to show that Module is available */
04705 #define __MSP430_BASEADDRESS_WDT_A__ 0x0150
04706 #define WDT_A_BASE             __MSP430_BASEADDRESS_WDT_A__
04707 
04708 SFR_16BIT(WDTCTL);                            /* Watchdog Timer Control */
04709 SFR_8BIT(WDTCTL_L);                           /* Watchdog Timer Control */
04710 SFR_8BIT(WDTCTL_H);                           /* Watchdog Timer Control */
04711 /* The bit names have been prefixed with "WDT" */
04712 /* WDTCTL Control Bits */
04713 #define WDTIS0                 (0x0001)       /* WDT - Timer Interval Select 0 */
04714 #define WDTIS1                 (0x0002)       /* WDT - Timer Interval Select 1 */
04715 #define WDTIS2                 (0x0004)       /* WDT - Timer Interval Select 2 */
04716 #define WDTCNTCL               (0x0008)       /* WDT - Timer Clear */
04717 #define WDTTMSEL               (0x0010)       /* WDT - Timer Mode Select */
04718 #define WDTSSEL0               (0x0020)       /* WDT - Timer Clock Source Select 0 */
04719 #define WDTSSEL1               (0x0040)       /* WDT - Timer Clock Source Select 1 */
04720 #define WDTHOLD                (0x0080)       /* WDT - Timer hold */
04721 
04722 /* WDTCTL Control Bits */
04723 #define WDTIS0_L               (0x0001)       /* WDT - Timer Interval Select 0 */
04724 #define WDTIS1_L               (0x0002)       /* WDT - Timer Interval Select 1 */
04725 #define WDTIS2_L               (0x0004)       /* WDT - Timer Interval Select 2 */
04726 #define WDTCNTCL_L             (0x0008)       /* WDT - Timer Clear */
04727 #define WDTTMSEL_L             (0x0010)       /* WDT - Timer Mode Select */
04728 #define WDTSSEL0_L             (0x0020)       /* WDT - Timer Clock Source Select 0 */
04729 #define WDTSSEL1_L             (0x0040)       /* WDT - Timer Clock Source Select 1 */
04730 #define WDTHOLD_L              (0x0080)       /* WDT - Timer hold */
04731 
04732 #define WDTPW                  (0x5A00)
04733 
04734 #define WDTIS_0                (0*0x0001u)    /* WDT - Timer Interval Select: /2G */
04735 #define WDTIS_1                (1*0x0001u)    /* WDT - Timer Interval Select: /128M */
04736 #define WDTIS_2                (2*0x0001u)    /* WDT - Timer Interval Select: /8192k */
04737 #define WDTIS_3                (3*0x0001u)    /* WDT - Timer Interval Select: /512k */
04738 #define WDTIS_4                (4*0x0001u)    /* WDT - Timer Interval Select: /32k */
04739 #define WDTIS_5                (5*0x0001u)    /* WDT - Timer Interval Select: /8192 */
04740 #define WDTIS_6                (6*0x0001u)    /* WDT - Timer Interval Select: /512 */
04741 #define WDTIS_7                (7*0x0001u)    /* WDT - Timer Interval Select: /64 */
04742 #define WDTIS__2G              (0*0x0001u)    /* WDT - Timer Interval Select: /2G */
04743 #define WDTIS__128M            (1*0x0001u)    /* WDT - Timer Interval Select: /128M */
04744 #define WDTIS__8192K           (2*0x0001u)    /* WDT - Timer Interval Select: /8192k */
04745 #define WDTIS__512K            (3*0x0001u)    /* WDT - Timer Interval Select: /512k */
04746 #define WDTIS__32K             (4*0x0001u)    /* WDT - Timer Interval Select: /32k */
04747 #define WDTIS__8192            (5*0x0001u)    /* WDT - Timer Interval Select: /8192 */
04748 #define WDTIS__512             (6*0x0001u)    /* WDT - Timer Interval Select: /512 */
04749 #define WDTIS__64              (7*0x0001u)    /* WDT - Timer Interval Select: /64 */
04750 
04751 #define WDTSSEL_0              (0*0x0020u)    /* WDT - Timer Clock Source Select: SMCLK */
04752 #define WDTSSEL_1              (1*0x0020u)    /* WDT - Timer Clock Source Select: ACLK */
04753 #define WDTSSEL_2              (2*0x0020u)    /* WDT - Timer Clock Source Select: VLO_CLK */
04754 #define WDTSSEL_3              (3*0x0020u)    /* WDT - Timer Clock Source Select: reserved */
04755 #define WDTSSEL__SMCLK         (0*0x0020u)    /* WDT - Timer Clock Source Select: SMCLK */
04756 #define WDTSSEL__ACLK          (1*0x0020u)    /* WDT - Timer Clock Source Select: ACLK */
04757 #define WDTSSEL__VLO           (2*0x0020u)    /* WDT - Timer Clock Source Select: VLO_CLK */
04758 
04759 /* WDT-interval times [1ms] coded with Bits 0-2 */
04760 /* WDT is clocked by fSMCLK (assumed 1MHz) */
04761 #define WDT_MDLY_32         (WDTPW+WDTTMSEL+WDTCNTCL+WDTIS2)                         /* 32ms interval (default) */
04762 #define WDT_MDLY_8          (WDTPW+WDTTMSEL+WDTCNTCL+WDTIS2+WDTIS0)                  /* 8ms     " */
04763 #define WDT_MDLY_0_5        (WDTPW+WDTTMSEL+WDTCNTCL+WDTIS2+WDTIS1)                  /* 0.5ms   " */
04764 #define WDT_MDLY_0_064      (WDTPW+WDTTMSEL+WDTCNTCL+WDTIS2+WDTIS1+WDTIS0)           /* 0.064ms " */
04765 /* WDT is clocked by fACLK (assumed 32KHz) */
04766 #define WDT_ADLY_1000       (WDTPW+WDTTMSEL+WDTCNTCL+WDTIS2+WDTSSEL0)                /* 1000ms  " */
04767 #define WDT_ADLY_250        (WDTPW+WDTTMSEL+WDTCNTCL+WDTIS2+WDTSSEL0+WDTIS0)         /* 250ms   " */
04768 #define WDT_ADLY_16         (WDTPW+WDTTMSEL+WDTCNTCL+WDTIS2+WDTSSEL0+WDTIS1)         /* 16ms    " */
04769 #define WDT_ADLY_1_9        (WDTPW+WDTTMSEL+WDTCNTCL+WDTIS2+WDTSSEL0+WDTIS1+WDTIS0)  /* 1.9ms   " */
04770 /* Watchdog mode -> reset after expired time */
04771 /* WDT is clocked by fSMCLK (assumed 1MHz) */
04772 #define WDT_MRST_32         (WDTPW+WDTCNTCL+WDTIS2)                                  /* 32ms interval (default) */
04773 #define WDT_MRST_8          (WDTPW+WDTCNTCL+WDTIS2+WDTIS0)                           /* 8ms     " */
04774 #define WDT_MRST_0_5        (WDTPW+WDTCNTCL+WDTIS2+WDTIS1)                           /* 0.5ms   " */
04775 #define WDT_MRST_0_064      (WDTPW+WDTCNTCL+WDTIS2+WDTIS1+WDTIS0)                    /* 0.064ms " */
04776 /* WDT is clocked by fACLK (assumed 32KHz) */
04777 #define WDT_ARST_1000       (WDTPW+WDTCNTCL+WDTSSEL0+WDTIS2)                         /* 1000ms  " */
04778 #define WDT_ARST_250        (WDTPW+WDTCNTCL+WDTSSEL0+WDTIS2+WDTIS0)                  /* 250ms   " */
04779 #define WDT_ARST_16         (WDTPW+WDTCNTCL+WDTSSEL0+WDTIS2+WDTIS1)                  /* 16ms    " */
04780 #define WDT_ARST_1_9        (WDTPW+WDTCNTCL+WDTSSEL0+WDTIS2+WDTIS1+WDTIS0)           /* 1.9ms   " */

04788 
04789 #define TLV_CRC_LENGTH         (0x1A01)       /* CRC length of the TLV structure */
04790 #define TLV_CRC_VALUE          (0x1A02)       /* CRC value of the TLV structure */
04791 #define TLV_START              (0x1A08)       /* Start Address of the TLV structure */
04792 #define TLV_END                (0x1AFF)       /* End Address of the TLV structure */
04793 
04794 #define TLV_LDTAG              (0x01)         /*  Legacy descriptor (1xx, 2xx, 4xx families) */
04795 #define TLV_PDTAG              (0x02)         /*  Peripheral discovery descriptor */
04796 #define TLV_Reserved3          (0x03)         /*  Future usage */
04797 #define TLV_Reserved4          (0x04)         /*  Future usage */
04798 #define TLV_BLANK              (0x05)         /*  Blank descriptor */
04799 #define TLV_Reserved6          (0x06)         /*  Future usage */
04800 #define TLV_Reserved7          (0x07)         /*  Serial Number */
04801 #define TLV_DIERECORD          (0x08)         /*  Die Record  */
04802 #define TLV_ADCCAL             (0x11)         /*  ADC12 calibration */
04803 #define TLV_ADC12CAL           (0x11)         /*  ADC12 calibration */
04804 #define TLV_ADC10CAL           (0x13)         /*  ADC10 calibration */
04805 #define TLV_REFCAL             (0x12)         /*  REF calibration */
04806 #define TLV_TAGEXT             (0xFE)         /*  Tag extender */
04807 #define TLV_TAGEND             (0xFF)         //  Tag End of Table

04809 /************************************************************
04810 * Interrupt Vectors (offset from 0xFF80)

04812 
04813 #pragma diag_suppress 1107
04814 #define VECTOR_NAME(name)             name##_ptr
04815 #define EMIT_PRAGMA(x)                _Pragma(#x)
04816 #define CREATE_VECTOR(name)           void * const VECTOR_NAME(name) = (void *)(long)&name
04817 #define PLACE_VECTOR(vector,section)  EMIT_PRAGMA(DATA_SECTION(vector,section))
04818 #define PLACE_INTERRUPT(func)         EMIT_PRAGMA(CODE_SECTION(func,".text:_isr"))
04819 #define ISR_VECTOR(func,offset)       CREATE_VECTOR(func); \
04820                                       PLACE_VECTOR(VECTOR_NAME(func), offset) \
04821                                       PLACE_INTERRUPT(func)
